	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 0, "ps3/s12/00/otaa18007", 256, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(5, 0, "ps3/s12/00/otab18009", 256, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(6, 0, "ps3/s12/00/otac18006", 256, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(7, 0, "ps3/s12/00/otad18006", 256, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(8, 0, "ps3/s12/00/otae18007", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "Ｋぇぇい！！」",
		   NULL, "KEEEIIIII!!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	PlaySE( 0, "wa_007", 56, 64 );
	DrawScene( "background/furiker_a", 50 );
	StartShakingOfWindow( 241, 40, 0, 2, 5*2, FALSE );
	StartShakingOfAllObjects( 241, 40, 0, 2, 5*2, TRUE );

	ModDrawCharacter(2, 2, "sprite/re1a_bikkuri_a1_", "1", 160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 0, FALSE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f0953d>レナ</color>", NULL, "<color=#f0953d>Rena</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s12/02/180200471", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……け、…圭一くんって、意外なところでも人気者なんだね…。」",
		   NULL, "\"K-Keiichi-kun è davvero benvoluto...\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacterWithFiltering(1, 3, "sprite/me1a_tohoho_a1_", "0", "maskleft", 7, -160, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 300, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	OutputLine(NULL, "「うちの町会もそうだけど…。",
		   NULL, "\"Persino il consiglio cittadino lo adora...", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 3, "ps3/s12/03/180300419", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "本人の与り知れぬところで評判が高いんだよ…。",
		   NULL, " trova consensi nei posti più strani...", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 3, "ps3/s12/03/180300420", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "同性に訴えるカリスマでもあるのかねぇ？」",
		   NULL, " e nutrono tutti un profondo rispetto nei suoi confronti.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DrawScene( "background/res5", 300 );
	ModDrawCharacterWithFiltering(2, 6, "sprite/si3_wink_a1_", "0", "maskleft", 7, -160, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 300, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s12/06/180600272", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「お店の子たちも、沙都子の事情に同情してくれてるみたいで、非番で近所の子が何人か行きたがってるみたいです。」",
		   NULL, "\"Alcune cameriere hanno detto di essere preoccupate per Satoko... e che quindi verranno a darci man forte quando avranno un momento libero.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacterWithFiltering(1, 2, "sprite/re1a_warai_a1_", "2", "maskright", 7, 160, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 300, TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "「すごいね、圭一くん……。",
		   NULL, "\"Keiichi-kun, sei incredibile...", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s12/02/180200473", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "本当に６０人を集めちゃった。",
		   NULL, " con questo siamo arrivati a circa 60 persone.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s12/02/180200474", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "あるいはそれ以上に集まるのかもしれない…。」",
		   NULL, " E forse supereremo addirittura l'obiettivo...\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DrawScene( "background/res5", 300 );
	ModDrawCharacterWithFiltering(2, 5, "sprite/ri1_def_a1_", "0", "maskright", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 300, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>Rika</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s12/05/180500664", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「…………これが、運命を打ち破ろうとする力なの…。」",
		   NULL, "\"...... è questo il potere in grado di sconfiggere il destino...?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	ModFadeOutBGM( 0, 1000, TRUE, 1 );

	CallScript( "&eye" );
	ModFadeOutBGM( 0, 1000, TRUE, 0 );
}
